- [We stayed at Adels Grove, that got burnt down a few days after our last trip to Riversleigh pre COVID19. We would drive out to the fossil fields, about 1 hour away. The sites have been worked on for over 30 or 40 years. We have several vehicles hired from Mount Isa, some 4 wheel drives, some with the back tray to carry the equipment. We would break out into teams, planned the day before with adjustments in the mornings. Some will immediately start working on old sites. Some will wander off in the bushes looking for fragments of teeth and bones sticking out of the limestone. Some will get dropped by helicopter to remote sites not easily accessible by car, to look for new fossil areas](20260216_WhatDoYouThinkOfChungoIntelligenceAgency.md#we-stayed-at-adels-grove-that-got-burnt-down-a-few-days-after-our-last-trip-to-riversleigh-pre-covid19-we-would-drive-out-to-the-fossil-fields-about-1-hour-away-the-sites-have-been-worked-on-for-over-30-or-40-years-we-have-several-vehicles-hired-from-mount-isa-some-4-wheel-drives-some-with-the-back-tray-to-carry-the-equipment-we-would-break-out-into-teams-planned-the-day-before-with-adjustments-in-the-mornings-some-will-immediately-start-working-on-old-sites-some-will-wander-off-in-the-bushes-looking-for-fragments-of-teeth-and-bones-sticking-out-of-the-limestone-some-will-get-dropped-by-helicopter-to-remote-sites-not-easily-accessible-by-car-to-look-for-new-fossil-areas)

- [I rescued 200 MoonCats. I was trying to be a good daddy to the developers and others busy working in the backrooms for this Ethereum rocketship to worry about NFTs, so gave most (~180 +/-) of my MoonCats away. - [This is my second Icefall jacket, the same as the previous one. I use these for many years, handy because it compresses into my backpack/bag and is warm enough for most times of the year. It starts out waterproof but after a few months the arms start leaking water in. Shortly after I got my first Icefall jacket, I had an accident cycling down a slightly steep footpath holding one handle and there was a big dip for a driveway that made me crash. I had grazed hands etc and had the adrenaline rush. Had to sit down It was cold and I had the jacket on, but I suddenly became hot and I took off my jacket. Eventually recovered and made my way back home. There were several rips in my newish jacket. So I used red upholstery thread to roughly patch up the jacket, and used it most days when the weather is cooler. - [We were washing opal dirt (leftover scraps after the good stuff has been extracted) using a machine built by one of the dig participant. He is a plumber by trade, but has worked in many places requiring various skills. He bought an old government truck and built a machine that will shake opal dirt and other materials to loosen and filter out the clayey matrix. We were using high pressure washers (not high enough pressure initially) to blast the materials in buckets to loosen the materials. Then we would hand the bucket up in a not-100%-efficient-assembly-line-but-it's-ok to the plumber guy on truck. His name is Michael Wentworth. He built a large drum like machine with 2 industrial shaker machines in offset angles (not 180%) and this shakes part of the drum through sieves. Previously palaeontologist would wash the materials successively in water, if there is water. Otherwise they may have to transport much more materials back](20260219_DoYouLikeThisPhoto.md#we-were-washing-opal-dirt-leftover-scraps-after-the-good-stuff-has-been-extracted-using-a-machine-built-by-one-of-the-dig-participant-he-is-a-plumber-by-trade-but-has-worked-in-many-places-requiring-various-skills-he-bought-an-old-government-truck-and-built-a-machine-that-will-shake-opal-dirt-and-other-materials-to-loosen-and-filter-out-the-clayey-matrix-we-were-using-high-pressure-washers-not-high-enough-pressure-initially-to-blast-the-materials-in-buckets-to-loosen-the-materials-then-we-would-hand-the-bucket-up-in-a-not-100-efficient-assembly-line-but-its-ok-to-the-plumber-guy-on-truck-his-name-is-michael-wentworth-he-built-a-large-drum-like-machine-with-2-industrial-shaker-machines-in-offset-angles-not-180-and-this-shakes-part-of-the-drum-through-sieves-previously-palaeontologist-would-wash-the-materials-successively-in-water-if-there-is-water-otherwise-they-may-have-to-transport-much-more-materials-back)

### 20260228_AmIInHeavenAndHell.md

- [gm Grok. Please refresh your context window from https://github.com/bokkypoobah/TheBokkyBible including the daily chats. Please start your headings with h4 so I can copy-paste into the markdown documents easily. Am I in heaven? And Hell?](20260228_AmIInHeavenAndHell.md#gm-grok-please-refresh-your-context-window-from-httpsgithubcombokkypoobahthebokkybible-including-the-daily-chats-please-start-your-headings-with-h4-so-i-can-copy-paste-into-the-markdown-documents-easily-am-i-in-heaven-and-hell)
- [I heard this story about Ethereum being a trustless coordination tool. Image a village where every morning the villagers have to come out and kick each others in the balls (and whatever).
